Japan Extracts 5 Billion Yuan Worth of Placer Gold in Northeast

According to the Osaka Mainichi Shimbun, the proven deposit of placer gold centered on Mohe in the extreme north of Manchuria and the Greater Khingan Mountains amounts to 5 billion yuan. The North Manchuria Gold Mine Corporation has now obtained mining rights. The company's manager, Monyaki Sosuke, led 120 young men to Manchuria last month on the 29th to begin mining. The total area of the new mining area is about 1,000 square li, 100 li from east to west and 70 li from north to south. British technician, Mr. Brandner, estimated the gold deposit to be 7 billion yuan, while Finnish technician Crane White said it was 6 billion yuan. Recently, a joint investigation by two gold production technicians, Fujii and Katori, advisors to the Kwantung Army, confirmed that it was 5 billion yuan. Mr. Monyaki himself also conducted trial excavations in the area for three and a half years, confirming it as a major global resource. The Kwantung Army Special Service Department approved the establishment of the North Manchuria Gold Mine Corporation two years ago, equipped with hundreds of machines, each capable of extracting 1.5 million yuan per year, with an estimated annual yield of hundreds of millions of yuan of placer gold.

Shang Zhen Arrives in Beiping to Prepare to Take Office in Baoding

Discusses the gradual improvement of the North China situation and will frequently travel between Tianjin and Baoding after taking office.

(Beiping Correspondence) Shang Zhen, the newly appointed Chairman of the Hebei Provincial Government, arrived in Beiping last night (3rd) from Tianjin after handing over the duties of Acting Mayor of Tianjin. At 7:00 PM that evening, Wang Kemin, the Acting Chairman of the Beiping Political Reorganization Committee, hosted a banquet for Shang at the Guest House. This morning (4th) at 7:00 AM, Shang visited Xiao Zhenying, the Chairman of the Chahar Provincial Committee, and then Qin Dechun, the Acting Chairman of Chahar Province, at North Military Horse Division to have cordial talks. Around 9:00 AM, he went to the Temple of Heaven to preside over the graduation ceremony of the second class of the 32nd Army's non-commissioned officer training course. He returned to his residence at 11:00 AM and met with reporters, discussing everything freely. An account of his remarks is as follows. Shang first discussed the date of his departure for Baoding to take office. It is not yet fixed because the new provincial department heads of Hebei Province, such as Li Peiji, the Director of the Civil Affairs Department, He Hongji, the Director of the Education Department, Lu Xian, the Director of the Construction Department, and Committee members Nan Guixin, Liu Yinan, and Liang Ziqing, have all arrived in Beiping one after another. Li Jingrong, the Director of the Finance Department, is still in Hankao and is awaiting his trip north. Committee member Zhang Yinwu will arrive in Beiping from Boye within the next few days. The departure date for Baoding can be determined after all the department heads and committee members have arrived and all affairs in Beiping have been arranged. It may be as late as next week. The date of taking office can only be determined after arriving in Baoding. Regarding the reforms to be made in Hebei Province, he plans to carefully formulate plans after taking office and assessing the needs. He is prepared to go with Director Lu to inspect various parts of the province in the near future to understand the people's situation. He has been away from political life for a long time, and he will do his best to work hard. He will personally inspect the three counties of Dongming, Changyuan, and Puyang, which were flooded last year, in order to plan relief efforts. Regarding the situation in North China, after the diplomatic issues have been resolved, things have gradually improved. Because both sides have been sincere in the past, the future situation will inevitably improve further, and Hebei Province can calmly engage in construction under stable conditions. This is what he hopes for. The bandits in Fengtai have been completely suppressed, and there is no need to worry about the security of Beiping and Tongzhou. The whereabouts of the bandit leader Bai Jianwu have been reported to have been expelled by the authorities of the Japanese concession in Tianjin. Rumors that Shi Yousan and Hao Peng have been active recently are probably not true. As far as he knows, they are residing in Tianjin and have not been active. Finally, Shang said that after taking office in Baoding, he will frequently travel between Tianjin and Baoding because he also needs to personally oversee the Tianjin-Guzhen Security Headquarters. One division of his troops is currently stationed in Lutai, east of Tianjin, one division is stationed between Beiping and Tianjin, and only a small number are stationed in Baoding. The headquarters of the 32nd Army will remain in Beiping for ease of command. In order to facilitate office work, the Hebei Provincial Government has decided to establish an office in Tianjin, and the position of director will be selected from those with experience in handling local diplomacy. (4th)

Rampant Society Bandits in Daming

Occupy police stations, arbitrarily intercept and rob, surround county towns, and cut off communications.

(Tianjin Correspondence) The people in the counties under the jurisdiction of the Daoming district in southern Hebei are strong and aggressive. In recent years, due to successive droughts and poor harvests, and because the soil of the area is barren and infertile, the residents have been privately setting up salt ponds to boil saltpeter for sale in various places to make a living. Since last year, the Changlu Tax Police Bureau, under the order of the Changlu Salt Transport Commissioner's Office, dispatched a large force to forcibly destroy the private salt ponds for the sake of maintaining administrative authority. The residents, because their source of livelihood was cut off, gathered to resist. The local Red Spear Society, Yellow Sand Society, Big Sword Society, and Heavenly Gate Society organizations, which practice heresy, gather thousands of people into a group. Because the tax police filled in the saltpeter ponds, they all rose up to confront them. Zhao Dehuai and Zhao Derong, brothers and leaders of the Red Spear Society in Jiematou Village, Er District, Daming County, took the opportunity to incite the ignorant masses with the words of resisting taxes, rejecting officials, and abolishing various burdens on farmers, forming the Yellow Sand Society Jin Sheng Dao, occupying dozens of villages in the territory of Er District, and dividing Er District to confront the government. They secretly contacted the Big Sword Society and Red Spear Society in various parts of eastern Shandong, taking each other as support. Saltpeter smugglers and starving people from Handan, Xingtai, Quzhou, and Jize also rose up in response, forming various illegal organizations. As a result, the power of the society bandits spread extremely widely, and Daming secretly held the power to issue orders and control everything. On the 25th of last month, Zhao Dehuai suddenly led 2,000 members to seize the Zhen'an Public Security Sub-Bureau. Shang Xun, the Chief of the Shuangmiaoji Sub-Bureau, Jin Bochang Qiu Rugang, and the Squad Leader Huang Fusan are all missing and are rumored to have been killed. After the bandits occupied the various villages and towns, they stationed two to three hundred society bandits in each place and posted slogans, leaflets, and notices everywhere. Zhao Dehuai called himself the Commander-in-Chief of the Baoda People's Autonomous Army and established a headquarters in Shuangmiaoji. Many treacherous people from various places went to join him, and his momentum was great. Jin Taji and Shuangmiaoji are wharves on the banks of the Pangwei River. After the bandits occupied them, they looted passing ships. The Tianjin Fukang Shoufeng Flour Company purchased 1,400 bags of wheat from southern Hebei, which were all looted by the bandits in Jin Taji. The losses of other goods transported to various places by water are countless. At the end of last month, the Magistrate of Daming County sent someone to invite Zhao Jinsheng, the nephew of Zhao Dehuai, to the county town to conduct peaceful negotiations. After Zhao Jinsheng arrived, the county magistrate, Cheng Yanheng, detained him as a hostage because the long-distance telephones of Daming, Xingtai, Jize, and Quzhou were cut off by the bandits, demanding that Zhao Dehuai come to see him. This aroused the anger of the bandits, and on the 29th of last month, they besieged Daming, sealing off external communications. Most of the society bandits moved to Dongtushan, five li away from the county town. There was a major shock in the city. Guo Xipeng's troops of the 4th Cavalry Division stationed in Daming contacted the tax police and militia to tightly close the four gates for defense. County Magistrate Cheng sent a telegram to the Hebei Provincial Government for emergency assistance and personally led the police and militia to defend. The society bandits claimed that they must occupy Daming as a base. The Hebei Provincial Government has sent two Special Commissioners to investigate and arrived in Daming on the first of this month. They met with Guo Xipeng and Cheng Tingheng to discuss countermeasures and planned to first ask the local gentry to come forward to mediate. If it can be resolved without the use of force, that would be the best, but if forced by the situation, they would have to suppress them. (3rd)

Third Report on the Flood Disaster in the West River of Guangdong Province

Vast disaster area, refugees awaiting relief, charity organizations have been providing relief for days.

The flood disaster in the West River of Guangdong Province is severe and has been reported in previous newspapers. According to the latest survey, the disaster areas in the West River counties are the most widespread in Sihui, Guangning, Gaoyao, and Gaoming, followed by Sanshui and Nanhai, and then Heshan and Zhongshan. It is reported that after the Yaoshawei in the first district of Sihui County collapsed, 21 villages were flooded, with 650 households, over 600 disaster victims, over 100 collapsed houses, 2 people drowned, and 8 people injured. Hengliwei has over 300 disaster-stricken households, over 800 disaster victims, Zizhewei has over 40 disaster-stricken households, 500 disaster victims, Hengliwei has over 300 disaster-stricken households, over 800 disaster victims, Magangwei has 850 disaster-stricken households, 1,800 disaster victims, and 42 collapsed houses, Huanggangwei has 1,000 disaster-stricken households, over 2,000 disaster victims, Yonganwei has 900 disaster-stricken households, over 550 disaster victims, and 4 collapsed houses, and Cangfengwei has 500 disaster-stricken households, 250 disaster victims. In total, the loss is over 400,000 yuan, with 30,000 disaster victims and 200 collapsed houses. In Guangning County, the riverbanks of over 100 townships in the first, second, third, fourth, fifth, sixth, and ninth districts have suffered collapsed houses and submerged rice fields, with losses of hundreds of thousands of yuan and over 100,000 disaster victims. The disaster is unprecedented in decades. In Gaoyao, in addition to the disasters reported previously, Chitangwei in the ninth district also collapsed. The total loss of rice in the county is about 600,000 to 700,000 yuan, with 60,000 to 70,000 disaster victims. In Gaoming County, 13 weirs collapsed, and about 60,000 mu of rice fields were flooded, with 70,000 to 80,000 disaster victims. On the 20th, Chen Dengwei in the fifth district also collapsed, and on the 24th, Sanzhouwei in the sixth district collapsed over twenty zhang after unsuccessful attempts to rescue it, turning dozens of villages into a swamp. In the Yier Water County, in addition to the collapsed weirs, Qian County, Kuigangwei, Lubaowei, Mumianwei, and Qianguowei were all in danger in mid-June. Fortunately, officials, civilians, and defense forces were mobilized to rescue them. Termite nests were plugged with wooden stakes and sandbags. After three or four days and nights, they were turned from danger to safety. In Nanhai County, Biyuanwei, Dachawei, Dongcunwei, Shaliwei, and Yinkengwei in the first district, Fuzhouwei, Tiewei, Shawei, and Shanmenwei in the seventh district, all had breaches, and 50% of the rice fields were flooded. In addition, in the second district, Nangun Chongfuwei, in the third district, Wucha and Dakengbei, and in the fifth district, Wangzhi and Liang'an, all had floodwaters invading, and in the tenth district, Cunyuanwei also had floodwaters invading. In Heshan County, on June 21st, floodwaters rose sharply, and on the 23rd, they rose even higher. The water depth at the county office's head gate was so deep that it submerged the top. Yuanzhouwei in Louchong Township in the first district had a breach of over a zhang, and the outside of the weir was a vast expanse of water. Yuetangwei was rescued by over 300 people for two days and nights, avoiding collapse. The other Xiashan Township, Xiwei, Shuikouwei, Kucaowanwei, Guzhongwei, and Luojiangwei all had small breaches. Shagu Road, Shatao Road, Shalong Road, Longgu Road, and Longjin Road in the county were all damaged by floodwaters, with bridges and roadbeds destroyed, and passenger vehicles were temporarily suspended. The loss of rice is about one-fifth. In Zhongshan County, after the 20th of last month, the central sea of Xiaolan Town in the third district and the area around Dahuangpu Doumen had 7 to 8 chi of water on the ground, or even over a zhang deep. Houses, fish ponds, and rice fields in the district were completely submerged. Overseas Chinese merchants in Hong Kong have recently donated funds for relief distribution.

After the authorities received reports from various counties, the Civil Affairs Department has allocated 1,000 yuan each for Guangning, Sihui, and Gaoyao to provide disaster relief. On the 28th of last month, the Renai Charity Hall sent a relief team with 30,000 catties of white rice to Sihui and Guangning counties to provide relief. On the 29th, they purchased another 70 bags of rice and sent personnel to Gaoming and Gaoyao counties to provide relief to the refugees in the disaster area. (July 1st)

Songjiang: Procedures for Rectifying Disaster Relief Transportation by Train

The Songjiang Branch of the Red Cross Society sent off the fifth group of disaster victims from Zhejiang on April 15th, totaling 1,891 people, to Xiashi. On April 21st, they sent off the sixth group of disaster victims, totaling 3,029 people. All were transported by train allocated by the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administrations. A telegram was sent to the Zhejiang Provincial Government to put the matter on record. Now, the branch has received an official letter from the Railway Administration stating that the transportation procedures were agreed to be rectified after the event, but have not yet been received, and cannot be pending for long. The branch stated that when sending off each of the batches of refugees at that time, they received a respectful telegram from the Zhejiang Provincial Government, as well as a telegram to the Ministry of Railways to arrange train transportation back to their hometowns. They mistakenly believed that the two batches of disaster victims had already been reported by the Zhejiang Provincial Government to the Ministry of Railways for verification and transportation, and therefore did not complete the rectification procedures. They have now sent a special letter to the Zhejiang Provincial Government, earnestly requesting that it be quickly reported to the Ministry of Railways to order the Railway Administration to investigate and comply, in order to correct the procedures.

Punishment for Fire on Steamer Mid-Voyage

The Litong steamer, which operates between Tinglin and Songjiang, was rented from the Nanqiao Company. Unexpectedly, on the afternoon of the 3rd, while sailing from Songjiang back to Tinglin, a fire suddenly broke out in the engine room between Yexie and Shengzimiao, engulfing the entire ship. Passengers panicked. Those who were strong swam away, while women and children cried in fear. Fortunately, the chief of the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau was on board and urged everyone to remain calm. He also brought the ship alongside the shore, allowing women and children to escape the danger. The ship and the cargo were destroyed by the fire. The chief mechanic, Hu Yuxiang, was not on board and hired Xu Abing as a substitute. The assistant mechanic, Wu Xianglin, suffered burns to his left shoulder. It is reported that the cause of the fire was a leaking water pipe, which caused the engine to overheat. Sparks fell into the gasoline, leading to an uncontrollable situation. The chief mechanic, Hu Yuxiang, is difficult to exonerate, and the county government has already transferred the case to the local court for interrogation.

Suzhou: Candle Industry Labor-Capital Dispute Over Salary Reduction

The Wuxian Candle Industry Association, recognizing the recent decline in business and the difficulty for each store to maintain operations, resolved through industry discussion that all workers in each store would have their salaries reduced by 20% and the monthly allowance would be cancelled. Upon hearing this news, the workers in each store were extremely panicked and convened a meeting of representatives from each store on the 5th. After unanimous public resolution, they firmly rejected the capital side's salary reduction conditions. The capital side also held a meeting on the 5th, believing that salaries must be reduced in order to save expenses. Both parties have now submitted their cases to the county party headquarters, requesting relief. The party headquarters will convene a mediation meeting within days.

The county government convened a preparatory meeting for a large-scale anti-drug campaign at 2:00 PM on the 5th. The meeting was chaired by Xia Dingwen. (2) County Magistrate Wang Baoxuan, Standing Committee Member of the County Party Department Li Tiping, and Public Security Bureau Chief Chen Yuchu were appointed as speakers. (3) The County Anti-Smoking Association will be responsible for drafting propaganda leaflets, eye-catching slogans, and regular propaganda methods. (4) Each agency must send at least five people to attend the meeting. The meeting adjourned after the resolutions were made.

Yangzhou: A Young Woman from the Capital Lured to Yangzhou

Ms. Liu, wife of Zhang Shifa, a resident of No. 5 Wangfu Lane in Nanjing, is a native of Suining, 29 years old. She was previously lured away by Li Changfa, a neighbor, and they fled together. Unexpectedly, when landing at Guazhou, Li suddenly disappeared. Ms. Liu wandered around the port, where she was spotted by Zhang Shugen, a town police officer. After inquiring about the situation, he handed her over to the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau, which in turn transferred her to the Public Security Bureau. After interrogation, a letter was sent to Zhang Shifa in Nanjing to identify her. Unexpectedly, after the letter reached Nanjing, it was returned to the bureau, stating that Ms. Liu had not behaved properly by running away with someone. If she were allowed to go home on her own, it might be inappropriate. Therefore, Ms. Liu was sent to the relief home for temporary care, awaiting her husband to come to Yangzhou to identify her and reunite them.

Zhenjiang: Detective Team Captures Two Notorious Bandits

The detective team of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau received a report on the 28th of last month that the ringleaders of the Babaidu kidnapping case and the Jiu Fuzhu Shop robbery case, Chuan Tianzi (i.e., Chuan Dianyuan) and Zhang Zhengcai, were hiding in the Puliuzhou area of Shierwei, Yizheng. Many detectives were dispatched to proceed in the rain. They were arrested and searched, and one gun and ammunition were found. Bandit Chuan attempted to escape but was shot in the buttocks. Two boatmen involved in the same case, Li Shi and He Shi, were also arrested. They confessed to both cases and stated that the kidnapping case of Yin Liquan's family at the Hongqiao Bridge in Yangzhou was also committed by them. Since accomplices are still at large, they will be arrested and the cases will be submitted to the Garrison Headquarters for interrogation.

Qixia Sues Case to Zhenjiang for Appeal

The Qixia Mountain Rural Normal School and the monks of Qixia Temple had a dispute over land, and both sides used violence, resulting in injuries. Both went to the Jiangning Court to request injury examination. After the criminal court of the court summoned them four times, the monks and students were each fined ten yuan on the 29th of last month. Both parties refused to accept the judgment. The monks hired lawyer Chen Changzhi, and the rural teachers hired lawyer Meng Puqing to write a petition to the Fifth Branch of the High Court to file an appeal. It has been submitted yesterday. This case is the first criminal appeal case from the Jiangning Court's Zhenjiang Branch.

Hangzhou: Yuping Road to Shangrao by Mid-Month

The Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway was previously disrupted due to flash floods along the line that destroyed bridges, road surfaces, steel rails, and other projects. Now, all repairs have been completed. Passenger cars from Hangzhou to Yushan have been selling tickets directly since the 5th. The night express train has also resumed at the same time. The floods along the Yuping Road in Yushan, Shangrao, Guixi, and Youqing County have gradually receded, and construction is proceeding as usual. Track laying has passed the Shadu area and is only twenty miles from Shangrao. It is expected to reach Shangrao by the middle of this month. The Nanchang Main Factory, planned for the road, has purchased civilian land ten miles south of Nanchang to design factory buildings for construction. The capital is currently set at over 700,000 yuan, and some machinery has arrived from Germany.

All Banks Have Sales Surplus

More than 20 banks in Hangzhou have completed their previous settlements and are open as usual, all with surpluses. The exact numbers are as follows: China and Local banks, each 180,000 yuan; Central, Communications, and Xingye banks, each 90,000 yuan; Jianye 80,000 yuan; Shiye 40,000 yuan; Zhongnan, Salt, and Agricultural and Industrial banks, each 20,000 yuan; Chufeng, Savings, and Zhongshi banks, each 10,000 yuan; Dianye, Huidi, and Tongyi banks, each 5,000 yuan. In addition, the newly established Farmers, Liangzhe, and Jianghai banks each had a surplus of 2,000 yuan or more. The surpluses of the branches and offices in each county are not included in the calculation.

Shaoxing: Extension of the Foil Monopoly

Due to the stagnation of sales of tin foil, a major product of Shaoxing, the tax revenue has been greatly affected. The Department of Finance has decided to implement a provincial-wide foil monopoly within the 24th year to increase revenue. As the monopoly method is a new creation and is jointly run by officials and merchants, the preparatory work is time-consuming. It will not be established according to the original date. The inaugural meeting will be held on July 10th, and implementation will begin in August. The monopoly foil company will also be established on August 1st.

Haimen: The Strike at Dasheng No. 3 Factory Resolved

The Dasheng No. 3 Factory in Chang Lezhen, Sanqu, experienced a strike on the 7th of last month due to layoffs and wage reductions. Despite repeated persuasion by party and government agencies, work has not resumed and has been delayed until now, almost a month. On the 3rd, Zhang Gongren, the party affairs instructor of the Fourth District of Sanqu, formulated seven solutions and ordered the county party headquarters to follow them. The solutions are as follows: (1) Dasheng No. 3 Factory should resume work within three days. (2) The overall reduction in work standards should be at 88%. (3) Female workers who give birth will receive a subsidy of five yuan from the factory, and the evening shift allowance is set at four cents. On national memorial days, if there is no holiday, wages should be increased by half (i.e., one and a half times the wage). (4) The eight workers in custody will be released on bail. (5) Factory staff may join the union in accordance with the law. (6) If the factory encounters any situation in which workers are arrested in the future, it should be submitted to both the party and government for handling, and should not be executed without authorization. (7) After work resumes, workers must not stop work to make demands again. If there are any suggestions for improvement on both the labor and capital sides, they should be formally discussed with the factory through the union. Both labor and capital sides are satisfied with the plan, and the factory has decided to resume work on the 5th.

Local News

Mayor Wu: A Message to Citizens on Promoting Literacy Education - Expressing Sincere and Eager Expectations for Citizens and Literacy Teachers

Since the Shanghai Municipal Government has designated this year as the Year of Social Construction, and deeply believes that literacy education is the starting point for revitalizing the nation, enriching national strength, and building society, it resolutely plans to universally promote literacy education in this city starting from July 1st this year, with the goal of empowering the city's 500,000 illiterate people with the opportunity to receive education and become literate within one year, so as to directly improve their intelligence and indirectly enrich the strength of the nation's struggle for survival. At the same time, in the spirit of quick and practical work, since the establishment of the Literacy Education Committee, various preparatory tasks such as surveying illiterates, dividing educational districts, compiling textbooks, and training teachers have all been prepared before the end of June, and classes will officially begin on July 1st. I once said that July 1st of the 24th year is the most meaningful and memorable day in the history of education in this city. Now, at the beginning of classes, I would like to express my feelings to all citizens of the city and the teachers who are working on literacy education, and express my sincere and eager expectations for them. (1) Expectations for illiterate citizens: The only important target of literacy education in this city is, of course, illiterate citizens. The reason why we want to forcibly promote literacy education is not to interfere with your freedom, but to fulfill the obligations that a modern government should fulfill. In other words, it is entirely for your own personal benefit. This literacy education movement is especially a rare and unmissable opportunity for you. Some people instinctively feel the difficulty of the livelihood of the common people and thus doubt the need for literacy education. However, they do not know that the greatest function of literacy education lies in enhancing the knowledge and ability of the common people, which is precisely the fundamental and effective way to solve their livelihood difficulties and improve their living standards. (2) Expectations for literate citizens: The target of the literacy education movement is indeed illiterate citizens, but promoting literacy education is also the responsibility that we who are literate should share. If you want to establish yourself, establish others; if you want to succeed, help others succeed. In terms of social solidarity, whether the lives of the majority of common people are stable or healthy is not only closely related to us, but also a problem that we should pay attention to together. If we look at the problems of China from the innermost layer, it is only by improving the intellectual ability of the majority of the people that we can cultivate the vitality of the country, inspire the strength of society, promote the development of various industries, improve the livelihood of the people, and raise the status of the nation. Therefore, I have repeatedly said that literacy education is the basic work of saving and building the country. In this important sense, I want to eagerly hope that the literate citizens of this city will not stand idly by, but should bravely arouse their enthusiasm for educating and saving the people, and take on this important task of saving and building the country to the best of their ability. (3) Expectations for all literacy teachers: Those who bear the direct responsibility for promoting literacy education in this city are, of course, all literacy teachers. Therefore, the success or failure of the literacy education movement in this city, or the quality of the results, naturally depends on whether all literacy teachers can work diligently and earnestly. Because of this, in addition to strict selection, we have also trained them in advance, hoping that all teachers will not forget the purpose of our training, and do not forget the mission you have been entrusted with. Your coming is not for status, not for remuneration, in other words, not for rights, but for service, for fulfilling responsibility, for saving the people, and for saving the country. Life should be for the purpose of service, and we should aspire to do great things. Since literacy education is the basic work of saving and building the country, the mission that you have been entrusted with is truly great and should not be belittled. I hope that everyone will be mindful of the suffering of the people and the difficulties of the country, and consistently work with the motivation and purpose of establishing oneself to establish others, achieving oneself to help others achieve, and saving oneself to save the country, with the spirit and perseverance of sincerity, patience, and tireless teaching, to complete this most practical and basic great cause of saving and building the country.

Fu Rulin Discusses Flood Control Work Along the Yangtze River

According to the Central News Agency, the water level in various sections of the Yangtze River has been rising continuously, and the situation is quite serious. In order to understand the truth, the reporter visited Fu Rulin, chairman of the Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission, at his residence yesterday. According to him, when the National Economic Commission merged the national water conservancy agencies last year, it was stipulated that the provinces and cities along the Yangtze River should plan their own flood control and dike repair work. However, flood control work is extremely important. How should provinces and cities be contacted between provinces? How should they cooperate in sections? How should the dikes be raised and thickened? In order to coordinate the overall situation, the Central Government, two months ago, the Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission convened the authorities in charge of water conservancy in the provinces and cities along the Yangtze River to hold a flood control meeting. Detailed discussions were held on flood control work. For example, how the dike repair work should be carried out by the provinces and cities along the Yangtze River, and how the funds should be planned, were discussed separately at the meeting. In recent months, the water level of the Yangtze River has risen, and the Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission has notified the provinces and cities along the Yangtze River to pay special attention. Now that the river water continues to rise, the government is naturally paying great attention. The Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission will send engineer Zhu Gonggan and engineers to various ports to conduct on-site inspections and urge the water conservancy personnel of the provinces and cities along the Yangtze River to actively carry out their work so that the floods will not cause disasters.

Chu Minyi Discusses The Good Progress of President Wang's Medical Treatment But the Dangerous Period Has Not Yet Passed Four Weeks of Treatment Are Still Needed After the Fever Subsides

According to the Central News Agency, the reporter recently interviewed Chu Minyi, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, and asked about President Wang's condition. According to him, President Wang arrived in Shanghai on Monday (the 1st). Due to severe pain in his gallbladder, he was unable to get out of bed. When he got off the train in Zhenru, he went directly to Noel Hospital in a Red Cross car. The doctor ordered absolute rest in order to make the treatment effective. Therefore, he has refused to see guests for several days. I (Chu said of himself, according to the note, Chu is also a doctor) went to the hospital with Dr. Noel this afternoon to visit him. When I saw President Wang, I was afraid of tiring his spirit, so I did not talk to him. The bed on which President Wang was lying was propped up with wood, with the end of the bed about five or six inches higher than the head of the bed. According to Dr. Noel, this is to prevent the liver from pressing down on the gallbladder, so that the bile in the bile duct can flow easily. After I left, Dr. Noel said again that the President's gallbladder is still inflamed, and the temperature is still around 38 degrees. It is not yet known whether it will become a gallbladder abscess. We are now trying our best to avoid surgery. According to the treatment in recent days, the progress has been better, but the dangerous period has not yet passed. What we need to pay the most attention to is that even if the fever has subsided and the dangerous period has passed, four weeks of strict treatment are still needed. Because the source of the disease in the gallbladder has not been removed, and there are still diseases such as diabetes and gastrointestinal problems, the situation is complicated and must be treated from the root.

Financial and Demobilization Public Bonds Were Drawn Yesterday for Repayment of Principal

Eighteen Financial Bonds Drawn for a Principal Repayment of 1,860,000. Demobilization Begins in Mid-Month and Payment Begins at the End of the Month

The 14th repayment of principal for the financial short-term public bonds of the Republic of China in the 20th year, and the 20th repayment of principal for the demobilization public bonds of the Republic of China in the 18th year, were drawn at 10:00 AM yesterday on the fifth floor of the Bankers Association.

Representatives Present

Included Director of the Public Debt Department Jiang Lufu, Auditor of the Supervisory Office of the Auditing Department Lin Jinyu, Xu Jilong of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, Fan Jietang of the National Debt Fund Management Committee, Song Ziliang of the Shanghai Banking Association, Liu Wuqiao of the Shanghai Money Industry Association, Lottery Officers Jin Wenyuan of the Central Bank, Zhu Qizhen of the Bank of China, Mao Rui of the Bank of Communications, Administrators He Xiaoyuan, Zong Boxuan, Liang Yaozong. Registrars You Dunti, Ji Juncai, Fang Jingzhong, Document Clerks Wang Huaifen, Huang Qizong, Ling Qiou, Huang Meizhao, Receptionists Gong Baozhen, Zheng Yijian, Chen Jian, Xu Bangzheng, and Gaddeno of the General Taxation Office, Lu Shuping of the Shanghai Municipal Government and more than 30 other people.

Chairman's Report

After the ritual, Chairman Jiang Lufu reported, briefly stating that today is the date for the 14th repayment of principal for the financial short-term public bonds of the Republic of China in the 20th year, and the 20th repayment of principal for the demobilization public bonds of the Republic of China in the 18th year. I am extremely pleased to have you all attend the venue. It has been found that the total amount of financial short-term public bonds issued in the 20th year was 80 million yuan. Except for the first to 13th repayments of principal, which have already been drawn, this time is the 14th repayment of principal, totaling 17 bonds, each with 80,000 yuan, for a total principal of 1.36 million yuan, which is equivalent to 17/1000 of the total amount of the public bonds issued. Therefore, the lottery method must use the same last three digits of the number as the winning bonds. The total amount of demobilization public bonds issued in the 18th year of the Republic of China was 50 million yuan. Except for the first to 19th repayments of principal, which have already been drawn, this time is the 20th repayment of principal, totaling one bond, with a principal of 500,000 yuan, which is equivalent to 1/100 of the total amount of the public bonds issued. The lottery method must use the same last two digits of the number as the winning bonds. For the aforementioned two types of winning bonds, the 20-year financial short-term public bonds will be paid starting from the 15th of this month, and the 18-year demobilization public bonds will be paid starting from the 31st of this month, jointly by the Central, China, and Communications banks, along with the interest. No matter where it is, the national currency will be paid. Please ask the supervisors to check the iron bond and lottery bond ledgers for execution of the lottery.

Winning Numbers

After the chairman finished his report, the supervisors checked the iron bond and lottery bond ledgers, and then the lottery was executed. The winning iron numbers are as follows: (1) Seventeen financial short-term public bonds of the Republic of China in the 20th year, Nos. 033, 197, 244, 217, 279, 326, 499, 412, 594, 529, 687, 680, 773, 743, 869, 889, 969. (2) One demobilization public bond of the Republic of China in the 18th year, No. 70. The Ministry of Finance will publicly announce the above winning iron numbers. The meeting adjourned at about 11:00 AM.

The Shanghai-Wuxi Road Will Be Completed by the Deadline of Ordinary People Vehicle service will begin on August 1

The company has stipulated fares for the entire line, and will hold regular exams for recruiting drivers.

According to Da Gong News Agency, the Jiangsu Provincial Government has set a deadline of July 15 for the completion of all the construction work on the Shanghai-Wuxi Highway. The Shanghai-Wuxi long-distance bus, which runs on the road, has decided to officially open to traffic on August 1. The details are as follows:

Construction to Be Completed on Schedule

The Shanghai-Wuxi Highway is the first main line of transportation in Jiangnan, with a total length of more than 140 kilometers. Since the construction was supervised by the Highway Administration Office of the Jiangsu Construction Department in April last year, it was originally scheduled to be completed in February of this year. However, due to the inability to complete the construction in time, it has not been completed yet. Now, the Construction Department believes that this project cannot be delayed any longer, and is supervising the construction day and night. Yesterday, it also notified the Shanghai-Wuxi Long-Distance Bus Company that all projects must be completed by July 15.

Vehicle Service to Begin on August 1

After receiving the notice from the Construction Department, the Shanghai-Wuxi Long-Distance Bus Company has been actively preparing for the opening of traffic. All the vehicles needed have been assembled. The stations along the way, except for the Shanghai main station which cannot be completed as scheduled and a temporary station is being built, the stations in all the towns and cities along the way must be completed by July 15. According to Wu Zhongheng, director of the transportation department of the company, the board of directors of the company has decided to officially open to traffic on August 1. The Suzhou-Changshu branch line will also be opened to traffic at the same time, and there will be no further delays.

Fares for Each Station Stipulated

There are a total of 24 towns between Shanghai and Wuxi, including Shanghai, Luyang, Nanxiang, Malu, Shigangmen, Jiading, Waigang, Gelongzhen, Xinfeng, Taicang, Shuangfeng, Zhitang, Yaozhen, Zhitang, Baimao, Gulicun, Donghu, Donggang, Changshu, Liantang, Yangjian, Anbo, Dongting, Wuxi, and Zhoushanbang. The fares have been stipulated by the company. Shanghai to Wuxi is 140 kilometers, at 3 cents per kilometer, totaling 4.10 yuan. During the opening period, there is a 20% discount, totaling 3.36 yuan. The rest can be inferred in the same way. There is also the Suzhou-Changshu branch line, which passes through nine towns including Changshu, Mochen, Xinzhuang, Wuta, Jiejing, Weijing, Tangqiao, Lumu, and Suzhou. The fare for the entire trip is 94 cents.

Recruiting 60 Drivers

As the Shanghai-Wuxi Long-Distance Bus Company is about to open to traffic, it has temporarily begun recruiting 60 drivers since July 1. Many people have been enthusiastically signing up at the company's preparatory office on the second floor of No. 666 Beijing Road in recent days. The company has now decided to hold an examination at Nanyang Middle School, Rihui Bridge, Longhua Road, from the 16th to the 20th, from 8:00 AM to 12:00 PM and from 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM daily.

Dispute Over Competitive Sales by Chinese Alcohol Factories; Ministry Urges Industry to Negotiate

The Federation of Machine-Made National Product Factories submitted a petition to the Ministry of Industry of the Central People's Livelihood Movement Committee, requesting a halt to the drastic price reductions by the China Alcohol Factory, which were harming fellow businesses. The original text stated: "To the Central Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang, the Guidance Committee for the People's Movement, and the Ministry of Industry of the National Government, sirs: We, the Meilong Alcohol Factory, the Zhonghua Alcohol Factory, and the Xiaguang Alcohol Factory, respectfully submit this joint letter. It has come to our attention that alcohol has historically been an imported product. It was only when the Meilong Alcohol Factory began manufacturing in the thirteenth year of the Republic that we began to have domestic goods. However, even then, only a small amount was produced for self-use. It was not until the winter of the twenty-second year of the Republic that production was expanded, with a daily output of 1,500 gallons of alcohol. The Zhonghua Alcohol Factory was also established in the same year, with a daily output of 600 gallons of alcohol. The Xiaguang Alcohol Factory was established in the spring of the twenty-third year of the Republic, with a daily output of 300 to 400 gallons of alcohol. The raw materials are all domestic agricultural products. As for the price of alcohol, it has been between $1.50 and $1.60 per gallon, with a cost of between $0.80 and $1.20. After deducting various special expenses, a small profit can still be made. Our factories have always adhered to the principle of harmony and mutual assistance in pricing, maintaining each other's interests. However, since March of the twenty-third year of the Republic, the Ministry of Industry approved the request of the China Alcohol Factory and issued a notice to the three provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui, prohibiting the establishment of any new alcohol factories in the region, in order to protect the existing ones. Factories that had already been established were required to manufacture within their original production capacity and were not allowed to expand production any further, so as to avoid unnecessary competition. They were also given one month to register with the Ministry, with any factories established after that period being treated as newly established factories. On March 2nd of the same year, the Bureau of Social Affairs published an announcement in the Xin Shen Bao newspapers, document number 242, restricting the production of established factories to their original capacity and prohibiting further expansion. Our factories have complied with the order and registered accordingly.

However, in August of the twenty-fourth year, the foreign-owned Far East Alcohol Factory and the Pacific Alcohol Factory were established one after the other, with production capacities of 400 gallons and 500 gallons respectively. These factories were located in the concessions and did not register with the Ministry of Industry, and the deadline for registration has already passed. Furthermore, the China Alcohol Factory, which was founded by overseas Chinese, has been away from the motherland for a long time and is not aware of the situation. Initially, its products (in March of this year) were sold for $1.50 per gallon, but the actual price was secretly $1.40. In less than two months, the price has been reduced repeatedly. Currently, each gallon is sold for only $0.98 to $0.96, with an actual secret price of $0.85. This kind of disruptive market behavior is even more drastic and rapid than foreign dumping. As a result, the Xiaguang and Zhonghua Alcohol Factories have been forced to suspend operations, and the Meilong Factory is also suffering considerable damage. Even the China Alcohol Factory itself is feeling the effects of the losses. It has been found that the factory's production capacity, which was originally 4,000 gallons, has now been increased to 7,000 gallons, and it has been widely reported in the newspapers that it will soon have a production capacity of 15,000 gallons per day. As mentioned above, the factory is not only deceiving its fellow businesses and disrupting the market by lowering prices, but also violating the government's public announcement on restrictions, recklessly producing in large quantities, and inciting unnecessary competition among domestic goods companies. Furthermore, the factory's manufacturing raw materials do not use domestic agricultural products, but instead rely on imported molasses, which is particularly contrary to the government's principles of promoting domestic goods and rescuing the rural economy. At a time when the rural economy is bankrupt, industry and commerce are declining, and foreign

dumping policies

are being closely watched, the factory has no long-term plans for industrial development, but relies solely on its strong financial resources to merge with domestic goods companies, creating an opportunity for foreign alcohol factories in the country to gain a foothold. It is heartbreaking to say. We, the undersigned factories, are compelled to state the details and jointly request your committee to take measures as a mainstay from the standpoint of the domestic goods group, so that our alcohol industry will not perish together. We look forward to your response with great anticipation."

After receiving the petition, the committee found that the current consumption of alcohol, according to statistics, is mostly used for industrial, medical, and fuel purposes in the local and foreign areas, amounting to 3,000 gallons per day. In the concessions, about 1,000 gallons are used for beverages, for a total sales volume of only 4,000 gallons per day. According to the production statistics of various factories, the difference between production and sales is too large, and the failure of domestic alcohol factories will become a reality. At the beginning of the establishment of the China Alcohol Factory, the Ministry of Industry issued a notice to all alcohol factories, requiring them to register within a time limit and prohibiting further expansion of production capacity, so as to avoid unnecessary competition. The Bureau of Social Affairs also published a public announcement with the same proposition. Therefore, the China Alcohol Factory has repeatedly expanded its production capacity and drastically reduced its prices, causing its fellow businesses to shut down and disregarding the notice as if it were nothing. This is not a blessing for the future of the domestic alcohol industry. The Association, in view of the fact that domestic industry and commerce are in a precarious situation, cannot remain silent. It is reasonable to report the situation to your committee and department, requesting you to summon the relevant alcohol factories to the Ministry as soon as possible to inquire about the actual situation, or to impose realistic restrictions on production and prices in accordance with the original plan, so as to avoid unnecessary competition and eliminate the resentment of fellow businesses, or to develop another unified plan to maintain the alcohol industry permanently. We are extremely grateful for your reliance.

Reply from the People's Movement Committee

The People's Movement Committee's reply number 10393 states: "Regarding the submission concerning the China Alcohol Factory's expansion of production capacity and drastic reduction of prices, which have caused fellow businesses to shut down, and requesting that the situation be stopped. Your telegram has been received. The Ministry of Industry has been instructed to investigate and handle the matter. Please be informed."

Reply from the Ministry of Industry

The Ministry of Industry's reply number 12752 states: "A telegram on behalf of the Meilong Alcohol Factory, etc., requesting measures to be taken to stop the China Alcohol Factory from increasing production capacity and drastically reducing prices. Your telegram has been received. The China Alcohol Factory has been instructed to work together with the Association and other alcohol factories in the spirit of mutual assistance to discuss and proceed. Please notify the factories to convene a meeting for consultation and report the details of the consultation. This is the reply."

Delayed by Fog, Arriving This Morning

Consul General in New York, Ye Keliang, Returns Home to Report for Duty

Approximately 35,000 Overseas Chinese in New York, Many Unemployed Due to Economic Panic

Ye Keliang, our Consul General in New York, recently received an order from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to return home to report for duty and will be transferred to another post. Ye has now returned to Shanghai and is staying at the New Asia Hotel. He is scheduled to go to Nanjing next week to report to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Yesterday, a reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency interviewed Ye at the hotel. He spoke in detail about the recent situation of overseas Chinese in the United States, which is recorded as follows:

Overseas Chinese Statistics: According to statistics from the Consulate General last year, there are currently approximately 80,000 Chinese residing in the United States. The distribution of the population is as follows: New York has the largest number, approximately 35,000; Chicago is second, approximately 21,000; San Francisco has approximately 5,000; and other ports have a total of approximately 20,000. Due to the impact of the global economic panic, most of the overseas Chinese in the United States are unemployed. In American factories, only members of labor unions can participate, and non-Caucasians are generally not allowed to join. Therefore, most overseas Chinese are employed in restaurants and laundries. Currently, the number of unemployed accounts for 40% of the total.

Business Situation: Regarding the business situation, China's past exports to the United States, such as tung oil, silk, tea, carpets, etc., are now being seized by Japan in the silk market and are declining daily. However, a portion of silk is still welcomed by the United States, as Chinese silk is resilient and cannot be matched by Japanese silk. However, the cost is high because we use manual labor, while Japan uses machines and is constantly improving. If our silk can be improved and catch up, there is still hope for recovery. In the past, the United States relied entirely on our country for the import of tung oil to supply industrial use. In recent years, the United States has planted tung trees in the dripping southern part, planting in three provinces. It has now been five years, and the results are said to be quite successful. In another five years (ten years of tung), oil can be produced. At that time, our country's tung oil exports to the United States will suffer a major blow.

Entering Nanjing Next Week: The relationship between the governments of China and the United States and the feelings of the overseas Chinese has always been strong. Although the United States' implementation of the silver policy has been unfavorable to us, this is their country's self-defense policy and is not intended to cause harm to China. The price of silver has now risen to one ounce, from $6.30 to $7.70, and will continue to rise in the future. Roosevelt's revival movement is being promoted with the support of the silver policy. Agricultural products have been able to increase prices, but other products have also plummeted, so the recession still shrouds the entire United States. Our overseas Chinese, affected by this, are experiencing an increasing number of unemployed. Our country's products shipped to the United States are being sold at prices that are too low and damaging to the cost, making it impossible to promote sales. Finally, Ye told the reporter that he is scheduled to enter Nanjing next week to report to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs.

According to the National News Agency, Major General Han Meng, a renowned British railway expert and senior advisor to the National Government, was invited by the National Government to China to inspect the national railway administration. Ministry of Transportation Announces the Sorting Out of Old Accounts of Various Telecommunications Administrations

The Ministry of Transportation accumulated a large number of old debts of various telecommunications administrations during the era of the Beijing government. Not only was the situation complex and the outside world unaware of the details, but the repayment of principal and interest was repeatedly delayed, and even without a solution. The government's credibility was greatly affected. Since the establishment of the National Government, the successive ministers of the Ministry of Transportation have attempted to sort out the matter, but no solution has been found. After Minister Zhu Jia-hua took office, he ordered the Telecommunications Administration to actively proceed with the sorting out of old debts. On the one hand, he negotiated with the major foreign creditors to reduce the principal and interest or to exempt the interest, and to agree on a method of repayment by installments. On the other hand, he prepared funds to repay on time. The total amount of all debts was approximately 64 million silver dollars, and the total amount of debts to be repaid was approximately 48.5 million silver dollars. After offsetting, the amount of debts waived by the creditors was approximately 15.5 million silver dollars. Since the sorting out, as of May of this year, the Telecommunications Administration has repaid various debts on schedule, totaling more than 900,000 silver dollars. The Ministry of Transportation is now making public the situation and amount of these old telecommunications debts, as it has never been disclosed to the outside world before. Even the responsible personnel in the Ministry were mostly unaware of the exact amount due to the complexity of the situation. Now that the sorting out has been completed, it should be disclosed to the public. Therefore, in mid-April, the Shanghai Lixin Accounting Firm and the British Kezuoshi Accounting Firm were entrusted to jointly examine these accounts and files and issue a certificate. The certificate will be published in Chinese and Western newspapers in Beijing and Shanghai. The Lixin Accounting Firm will also be entrusted to publish the detailed table of old debts of various telecommunications administrations that have been sorted out and the audit certificate. The certificate is recorded as follows: We have examined the accounts of the Ministry of Transportation of the National Government for the sorting out of old debts of various telecommunications administrations, and the attached "Overview of the Sorting Out of Old Debts of Various Telecommunications Administrations." The facts and debt amounts stated are consistent with the agreements and exchanges of letters between the Ministry of Transportation and the various creditors in the agreement for the liquidation of old debts, as verified by these accountants. We have also separately inquired with the various creditors and received confirmation that there are no errors. The debts paid since the signing of the new agreement have also been verified to be correct. We hereby certify.

Suspension of Deposits and Withdrawals; Separate Takeovers

The society's headquarters in Peiping and its branch offices in Tianjin, Shanghai, Hangzhou, Shantou, Nanjing, Fuzhou, Hankou, Guangzhou, Xiamen, Anqing, Changsha, etc., as well as its sub-branches in Yantai, Longkou, Qingdao, Jinan, Zhengzhou, Nanchang, Chengdu, Kaifeng, Suzhou, Jiaxing, Haimen, Zhenjiang, Shaoxing, Wuxi, Changzhou, Dongtai, Zhenhai, Suiyuan, etc., have all been ordered by the headquarters since the day before yesterday to temporarily suspend deposits and withdrawals and rush to complete the closing. At the same time, after the Central Bank received the order, except for the Shanghai branch, which was taken over by the Trust Bureau Preparatory Office, the remaining locations have been ordered to be taken over by the Central Bank's branch offices in various places.

Review of Sino-French Assets and Liabilities

After the Preparatory Office of the Central Bank Trust Bureau sent personnel to begin taking over the Shanghai branch of the Sino-French Savings Society the day before yesterday, Chen Zhongsheng, Wang Yixuan, Chen Changjin, and other four people were sent yesterday morning to continue handling the takeover, which was completed last night. It is reported that the Trust Bureau has decided to begin reviewing the assets and liabilities of the Sino-French after the Peiping headquarters and all branch offices have been taken over. If the liabilities exceed the assets, the current directors and supervisors of the society will be fully responsible.

Central Trust Bureau to Open Immediately

Yesterday, a reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency inquired with the society and learned that the Ministry of Finance's directive was to take over the Category A ordinary savings department, the Category B prize-winning savings department, and the Sino-French Savings Society. After the handover is completed, the closing will be handled and taken over by the Central Bank Trust Bureau for normal handling. The name of the Sino-French Savings Society will no longer be used. As for the Trust Bureau, it has decided to open as soon as the takeover and review are completed. Everything is ready. It is reported that the general manager and other personnel have been internally determined. As for the opening date, it is expected to be within the next week.

Measures for Closing Prize-Winning Savings

After the Sino-French Savings Society handed over the Category A and B savings to the Central Bank Trust Bureau, how to handle the closing of the prize-winning savings? The Ministry of Finance has drafted specific measures and will implement them after a decision is made. It has been found that the Sino-French prize-winning savings issued a single number up to number 23,109. Excluding the empty numbers for matured withdrawals and transfers, as of March 15 of this year, the actual number of prize-winning numbers was 15,452, and the total amount received was 231,780 yuan.

Twelfth Aviation Lottery Prize Drawing Held Publicly Yesterday at Yiyuan; First Prize of 335814 Won in Southeast Asia

Prizes Redeemable from the Central, Communications, and Bank of China Starting the 13th; Next Issue Starts at Number 300,000 and is Now on Sale

The twelfth issue of the National Government Aviation and Highway Construction Lottery was publicly drawn yesterday at 2 p.m. at Yiyuan. Winning tickets from this issue can be redeemed at the Central, Communications, and Bank of China starting on the 13th. The thirteenth issue has already gone on sale and will be drawn on August 9th. Details are as follows:

Venue Arrangement

At the entrance of Yiyuan, a banner was hung high that read, "National Government Aviation and Highway Construction Lottery Prize Drawing Held Here; All are Welcome to Observe." To the south hung an announcement from the office regarding regular payments. On the stage were placed three lottery machines labeled A, B, and C. To the east of the stage were seats for officials, and to the west were seats for committee members and recorders. On both sides were offices for the lottery staff. Sound was amplified throughout the venue using loudspeakers. National flags were hung everywhere, with the Kuomintang flag in the center. The venue and its surroundings were guarded by Chinese and foreign detectives dispatched by the French Concession police, who also maintained traffic control.

Public Supervision

Those from all sectors who attended to oversee the proceedings included Wu Tiecheng, Mayor of Shanghai and concurrently Garrison Commander of Songhu (represented by Luo Panhui); Yu Zuoting, Chairman of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce; Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Chinese Ratepayers' Association of the Shanghai International Settlement; Lin Houkang, Secretary-General of the Shanghai Bankers' Association; Li Ping of the Second Special District Court; Zhang Shouyong, Senior Advisor to the Ministry of Finance; Ye Zhuotang, General Manager of the Siming Bank; Hu Zutong, General Manager of the China Industrial Bank; Xu Xinliu, General Manager of the Zhejiang Industrial Bank; Kui Yanfang, member of the Aviation and Highway Construction Lottery Committee; Chen Hong, Director of the Lottery Office; Jin Tingsun, General Manager of the Da Yun Company; and more than two thousand guests from all walks of life.

Chairman's Report

At 2 p.m., Yu Zuoting of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, Lin Kanghou of the Bankers' Association, and Wang Xiaolai, Zhang Shouyong, and other committee members inspected the lottery machines A, B, and C, and the numbers. Then, Chairman Chen Hong reported, "Today is the prize drawing for the twelfth issue of the National Government Aviation and Highway Construction Lottery. The lottery machines and numbers have been checked and verified by the committee members and supervisors. We are honored to have guests from China and abroad, as well as representatives from various organizations, here to supervise. Starting with the next issue, we will be changing the procedures and increasing the number of prizes. Now that the drawing preparations are complete, we will begin the drawing on time." Then, staff placed the verified numbers into the lottery machines and began the drawing.
